 What has been the history of the Nashik Lok Sabha seat
 
 
 nasik loksabhaa seat par sabase pehle 1952 main congress ne jeet hasil kii thi
 Yes
 ech deshpandey saansad chune gaye the
 After this, in 1957 Bhaurao Kishenji Gaikwad won elections from the Schedule Caste Federation
 1962 main dobaaraa ji
 H
 Deshpande became an MP by winning the election
 lekin unke nidhan ke baad 1963 main yahaan dobaaraa upachunaav hue
 Yashwant Rao Chavan was elected as an MP
 bataa den ki yashavanth raav chavaan maharashtra ke pehle mukhyamantri the, wo up-pradhanmantri bhi rahe
 In the subsequent elections in 1967, B
 aar kawade saansad bane, wo 1971 main dobaaraa jite
 In 1977, the victory of the Congress was broken by Vitthal Rao Hande
 wo shetakari kaamgaar paksh kii tikat se saansad chune gaye
 But the Congress returned in the 1980 election
 pratap raav vaagh saansad bane
 After that, in 1984, Muralidhar Mane won elections from the Congress
 jab pehali baar jiti bijepi
 
 
 The BJP won the Nashik Lok Sabha seat for the first time in 1989
 daulataraav aher saansad chune gaye
 But in the same year, the equation changed here and the Congress returned in the 1991 elections
 shivasena or ensipi kii entry
 
 
 
 1990 ke dashak main congress kii pakad nasik loksabhaa seat par kamjor padane lagi
 The effect of which appeared in the 1996 Lok Sabha elections
 yahaan shivasena ne pehali baar jeet hasil kii
 Rajaram Godse was elected MP
 lekin 1998 ke chunaav main congress kii waapas entry hui or madhav patil chunaav jite
 After this, the Congress was completely eliminated from the Nashik Lok Sabha seat
 1999 main shivasena ke uttamrao dhikale chunaav jite
 Then in 2004 NCP came to power for the first time here
 devidas aanandarav pingale chunaav jite
 In 2009 NCP managed to win the election again
 chagan bhujabal ke bhattije samir bhujabal saansad bane
 Then after the 2014 Lok Sabha elections Hemant Godse of Shiv Sena won here
 kya he vidhansabha siton kii sthiti

 You all know that Bhai Dooj is a festival of reverence and trust of sisters towards brothers
 is parv ko har saal karthik maas ke shukla paksh kii dwitiya tithi ke din hi manaaya jaataa he
 But very few people know about the reason for celebrating it
 darasal, bhai-bahan ke sneh kaa pratik yah parv deepawali ke do din baad manaaya jaataa he
 It is also called Yama Dwitiya
 isi vajah se is parv par yama dev kii puja kii jaati he
 According to the belief, one who worships Yama Dev does not fear premature death
 hinduonke baaki tyoharon ki tarahyah tyohaar bhi paramparaon se judaa hua he
 On this day, sisters wish their brother a long life by applying tilak and giving him a gift
 badale main bhai apni bahan ki raksha kaa vachan detaa he
 Eating a brother's house at his sister's day is particularly auspicious
 mithila nagari main is parv ko aaj bhi yamadvitiya ke naam se janaa jaataa he
 On this day rice is applied in both hands of brothers
 saath hi kuch sthanon main bhai ke haathon main sindur lagane kii bhi parampara dekhi jaati he
 After applying vermilion and rice paste in the hands of brother, five betel leaves, betel nut and silver coin are placed on it, chanting mantra for the brother's longevity by pouring water over it
 bhai apni bahan ko uphaar dete he
 According to a mythological belief about the beginning of Bhai Dooj, such as Bhai Dooj, Yamuna had fasted for the long life of his brother Yamraj on this day, and fed him the food of Annakoot
 katha ke anusaar yama devtaa ne apni bahan ko isi din darshan diye thea
 Yam's sister Yamuna was extremely distraught to meet her sister
 apane bhai ke darshan kar yamuna behad prasann hui
 Yamuna was happy and paid a lot of respect to her brother
 yama ne prasann hokar use vardaan diya ki is din agar bhai-bahan donon ek saath yamuna nadi main snaan karegein, to unhen mukti praapt hogi
 For this reason, bathing in this Yamuna river with brother and sister is of great importance
 iske alaava yama ne yamuna ne apane bhai se vachan liya ki aaj ke din har bhai ko apni bahan ke ghar janaa chahie
 Since then, the practice of celebrating Bhai Dooj has been going on
 bhai dooj kaa mahatvayah parv bhai-bahan ke bich sneh ke bandhan ko or bhi majboot karata he
 According to Indian tradition, after marriage, the girl has to come to her house, maiden
 maayke kii ore se bhi parivaar ke sadsy kabhi-kabhaar hi usase milane ja pate hai
 In such a situation, brothers should not be indifferent to their sister, always have affection for her, let her know the sister's happiness: sorrow
 bhai apni bahanon kii upeksha na karen, or donon ke sambandh madhur bane rahen
 The festival of Bhai Dooj is celebrated with this sentiment
 kaise manaaen bhai dooj kaa tyohaar- bhai dooj parv par bahanen praat: snaan kar, apane isht dev kaa pujan karti he
 She prepares chowk with rice flour
 is chowk par bhai ko baithaaya jaataa he
 And their hands are worshiped
 bhai kii hatheli par bahanen chaaval kaa ghol lagaati he
 After putting vermilion on it, water is released on the hands slowly by placing pumpkin flowers, betel nut, mudra etc
 on the hands
 - kahin-kahin is din bahanen apane bhaaiyon ke maathe par tilak lagaakar unki aarti utaarti hai or phir hatheli main kalava baandhti hai
 To sweeten the mouth of the brother, the brothers feed makhan-mishri
 sandhya ke samay bahanen yamraj ke naam se chaumukh diya jalaakar ghar ke baahar diye kaa mukh dakshin disha kii ore karke rakh detii hai

 " Sibal said, "but people are not aware of the way judges are appointed
 " He said, "there is no information or transparency in how the judges are elected because the right to information does not apply to them
" nyaaypalika kaa jo kathan kaaryakari par anivaary rup se lagu hota he vah nyaaypalika par bhi anivaary rup se lagu ho
 " sibbal ne kaha ki nyaayadhishon kii niyukti ko kargar banane kaa samay aa gaya he or niyukti kii arhata vistaar main tay kii jaaegi
 Earlier, taking part in the discussion, Leader of Opposition Arun Jaitley said that the bill for executive arrangements should be submitted to the Parliamentary Committee for the appointment of judges at a higher level in the judiciary
 jetali ne kaha ki vidheyak ek 'vidhayika kii ullekhneey kriti' he or isaki sansad kii sthaayee samiti dwaara samiksha jaruri he
 The comments unhone kaha, "ham is vidheyak ke vichaar kaa samarthan karte hai
 The standing committee will hear the favor of various participants, all should be allowed to give their views
 " Jaitley said that in the current collegium system of the Supreme Court, the judges included in the committee prefer their choice
 rajyasabha main netaa pratipaksh or bhartiya janata party (bhaajapa) sadsy arun jetali ne sarkaar ko 1993 se purv kii paddati main lautne ke khilaaf khabardaar kiya or vidheyak ko sansad kii sthaayee samiti ke hawaale karne kaa suzav diya
 Sibal underlined the need to streamline the appointment of judges at higher levels in the judiciary and restore the balance of independence of the High Courts
 unhone kaha, "nyaayadhishon kii niyukti main santulan behaal karne kii jarurat he or nyaayadhishon kii niyukti main kaaryakari kii vyavastha honi hi chahie
 " unhone kaha ki sadan main samvidhan sanshodhan vidheyak isliye pesh kiya ja rahaa he kyonki 'maujuuda pranali kaam nahin kar rahi he
 ' sibbal ne kaha ki ucch nyaayalayon kii nyaaypalika kaa 'najuk swatantraaa santulan' sarvocch nyaayalay ke collegium se vikshubdh he
 The collegium headed by the Chief Justice of the country consists of senior judges of the apex court
 unhone kaha, "ucch nyaayalayon ko sarvocch nyaayalay se swatantra mana jaataa he, sahyogi nahin
 Now the judges of the High Courts look to the judges of the Supreme Court for their appointment
 isse desh main ucch nyaayalayon kii najuk swatantraaa baadhit hoti he
 " sibbal ne kaha ki sarkaar 1993 se purv kii us sthiti ko waapas nahin laana chaahati jab nyaayadhishon kii niyukti main kaaryakari akele faisla letaa tha

 He said, "there is a need to restore balance in the appointment of judges and there should be a system of executive in the appointment of judges
 " He said that the Constitution Amendment Bill is being introduced in the House because 'the current system is not working
 ' Sibal said that the 'delicate liberty balance' of the judiciary of the High Courts is disturbed by the collegium of the Supreme Court
 desh ke pradhan nyaayadhish kii adhyakshata vaali collegium main sheersh adaalat ke varisht nyaayadhish shaamil hote hai
 He said, "high courts are considered independent of the Supreme Court, not allies
 ab ucch nyaayalayon ke nyaayadhish apni niyukti ke liye sarvocch nyaayalay ke nyaayadhishon kii taraf dekhte hai
 This hampers the fragile independence of the High Courts in the country
 " Sibal said that the government did not want to bring back the situation before 1993 when the executive took the decision alone in the appointment of judges
 sarkaar is disha main sammilit prayaas chaahati he

 vahiin is dauraan 80 suraksha balon ke jawan sarvocch balidaan dete hue shahid ho gaye
 In 2017 itself, 40 civilians also lost their lives in terrorist attacks
 grih mantralayadvara die gaye aankade ke mutabik pichley 3 saalon main sabase zyada 2017 main hi aatanki ghatnaayen hui, jisamen 342 baar aatankwaadiyon ne suraksha balon par hamalaa kiya
 At the same time, in 2016, 322 terrorists have attacked the security forces, in 2015, only 208 times terrorists targeted the security forces in different places
 is dauraan surakshabalon ne kashmir ghati main akele 2017 main hi 213 aatankwaadiyon ko dher kiya
 Whereas in 2016, only 150 militants were killed by the security forces
 pichley saalon kii apeksha 2017 main sabase zyada aatankwaadiyon ko surakshabalon ne maar giraae hai
 Last year, security forces in the Kashmir Valley carried out operations in all districts of All Out Kashmir, which is continuing this year
 oparation ol out kii safalataa yah thi ki kashmir ghati main aatankwaadi naa to seemaa paar se ghuspaith kar paa rahe the
 At the same time, the terrorists who were infiltrating the Kashmir valley were being piled up there
 yahi vajah he ki saal 2017 main pichley 3 saalon main sabase zyada 213 aatankwaadiyon ko surakshabalon ne oparation ol out ke tahat dher kiya
 However, despite this, Pakistan's intelligence agency ISI is continuously carrying terrorists from across the border on the launching pad to infiltrate terrorists into India
 in aatankwaadiyon ko aadhunik hathiyaaron ke saath-saath GPS system se bhi trend kar pakistan border par lekar aa rahaa he
 According to intelligence received by Aaj Tak, 386 terrorists are presently on the launching pad of cross-border Pakistan, who have been seated on different launching pads by Pakistan's intelligence agency ISI and Pak Army
 sutara bataate hai ki in aatankwaadiyon ko paak army kii special oparation team ne trend kiya he, joki bharat ke khilaaf badi vaardaat ko anjaam dene main sakasham he

 can
 bijepi ke pradhanmantri pad ke ummidavaaranarendra modine centre sarkaar ko galat nitiyaan banane ke liye jimmedaar tehraaya or congress par joardaar hamalaa kiya

 jhunjhunu jile ke khetadi main ek raily ko sambodhit karte hue narendra modi ne kaha ki nitigat vifaltaa ke kaaran kaarkaane band ho rahe hai

 kya he itihaas?1908-saal 1908 main mahilaayein apane adhikaron ko lekar aawaaj uthaa rahi thim

 Russian women celebrated International Women's Day for the first time on the last day of February and recorded their opposition to the First World War

 tippaniyan SEBI has said that investors will get electronic statement about their holdings in such accounts free of cost

 niveshkon ko aise dimet khaaton se koi bhi nikasi hone par esemes ke jariye jaankaree di jaaegi
 According to the SEBI circular, investors will be able to hold shares up to Rs 2 lakh in such accounts, but the maximum fee will be Rs 100 per annum for an amount above Rs 50,000
 iske anusaar agar in khaaton main rakhane vaale sheyaron kaa mulya 50,000 rupee tak hota he to dimet khate par salanaa rakrakhaav shulk nahin lagegaa
 SEBI has proposed to introduce this facility on the lines of no frill accounts opened in banks
